***progressief.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:progressief.html>progressief</a> (27472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>Probably</a> borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">progressif</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōgressīvus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:progressief.html>progressief</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:progressief.html>progressiever</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">progressiefst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>progressive, pertaining <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> favouring left-leaning, emancipatory <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> innovative <a href = vnd.unilang:politics.html>politics</a>, pertaining <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> supporting progressivism <span class="defdate">[<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> 19th <a href = vnd.unilang:c.html>c</a>.]</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:projectiel.html>projectiel</a> (22738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">projectile</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>prothese</a> (33106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:late.html>Late</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prothesis</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span>; cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>Prothese</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>prothese</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:now.html>now</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:common.html>common</a>) <span class="Latn" lang="en">prosthesis</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a> <span class="Latn" lang="fr">prothèse</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>prothese</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothesen.html>prothesen</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:protheses.html>protheses</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>prothesetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:provincie.html>provincie</a> (8749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:provincie.html>provincie</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōvincia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:territory.html>territory</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:under.html>under</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roman.html>Roman</a> domination; <a href = vnd.unilang:official.html>official</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duty.html>duty</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:office.html>office</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:charge.html>charge</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:province.html>province</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*prōw-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:right.html>right</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:judge.html>judge</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:master.html>master</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language"><a href = vnd.unilang:gothic.html>Gothic</a></a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍆𐍂𐌰𐌿𐌾𐌰</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">frauja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:lord.html>lord</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:master.html>master</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">frēa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruler.html>ruler</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:lord.html>lord</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:king.html>king</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:master.html>master</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
